(***************************************************************************************

 The existential quantifier in regular categories

 Suppose that we have a regular category. Following the interpretation of quantifiers as
 adjoints, then the existential quantifier is given by the left adjoint of the pullback
 functor. We show that in the displayed category of monomorphisms such left adjoints
 exists, which allows us to interpret the existential quantifier in regular categories.

 For ordinary morphisms, the left adjoint to pullback gives rise to dependent sums. For
 them, the left adjoint always exists, and it is constructed by taking the composition.
 The construction for monomorphisms is similar, because again we take the composition.
 However, the composition of a monomorphism with an arbitrary morphism is not guaranteed
 to result in a monomorphism, and thus we factorize the composition as an epimorphism
 followed by a monomorphism. The inclusion of the image gives the existential quantifier.

 The main work lies in proving the stability of the existential quantifier under
 pullback. The main steps are described throughout the proof.

 Content
 1. Interpretation of the existential quantifier
 2. Stability
 3. Dependent sums in the displayed category of monomorphisms

 ***************************************************************************************)
Require Import UniMath.Foundations.All.

#[local] Opaque regular_category_epi_mono_factorization.

Section MonoCodomainLeftAdj.
  Context {C : category}
          (HC : is_regular_category C).

  Let PB : Pullbacks C := is_regular_category_pullbacks HC.
  Let HD : cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C) := mono_cod_disp_cleaving PB.

  (** * 1. Interpretation of the existential quantifier *)
  Section ExistentialQuantifier.
    Context {y₁ y₂ : C}
            (f : y₁ --> y₂)
            (xg : C /m y₁).

    Let x : C := mono_cod_dom xg.
    Let g : Monic _ x y₁ := mono_cod_mor xg.

    (**
       The factorization
     *)
    Let im : C
      := pr1 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC (g · f)).

    Let e : x --> im
      := pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC (g · f)).

    Let He : is_strong_epi e
      := is_strong_epi_regular_epi
           (pr1 (pr222 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC (g · f)))).
    Let m : Monic _ im y₂
      := make_Monic _ _ (pr12 (pr222 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC (g · f)))).
    Let p : g · f = e · m
      := pr22 (pr222 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC (g · f))).

    (**
       The existential quantifier
     *)
    Definition mono_codomain_exists
      : C /m y₂
      := make_mono_cod_fib_ob m.

    
C: category
HC: is_regular_category C
PB:= is_regular_category_pullbacks HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving PB: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
y₁, y₂: C
f: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xg: C /m y₁
x:= mono_cod_dom xg: C
g:= mono_cod_mor xg: Monic C x y₁
im:= pr1
  (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC
     (g · f)): C
e:= pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC
        (g · f)): C ⟦ x, im ⟧
He:= is_strong_epi_regular_epi
  (pr122 (pr2
            (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC (g · f)))): is_strong_epi e
m:= make_Monic C
  (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC (g · f)))
  (pr122 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
                  HC (g · f)))): Monic C im y₂
p:= pr222 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC (g · f))): g · f = e · m
C /m y₁ ⟦ xg, mono_cod_pb PB f mono_codomain_exists ⟧

    Defined.

    Context {zh : C /m y₂}
            (φ : xg --> mono_cod_pb PB f zh).

    Let z : C := mono_cod_dom zh.
    Let h : Monic _ z y₂ := mono_cod_mor zh.
    Let φf : x --> mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f zh) := mono_dom_mor φ.
    Let q : φf · PullbackPr2 _ = g := mono_mor_eq φ.

            (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization

q:= mono_mor_eq φ: φf · PullbackPr2 (PB y₂ (pr11 zh) y₁ (pr21 zh) f) =
g
e · ?g = ?f · h

  (** * 2. Stability *)
  Section Stability.
    Context {x₁ x₂ x₃ x₄ : C}
            {s₁ : x₂ --> x₁}
            {s₂ : x₃ --> x₁}
            {s₃ : x₄ --> x₃}
            {s₄ : x₄ --> x₂}
            {p : s₄ · s₁ = s₃ · s₂}
            (Hp : isPullback p)
            (yg : C /m x₂).

    (**
       We use the following abbreviations.
     *)
    Let P : Pullback _ _ := make_Pullback _ Hp.
    Let y : C := mono_cod_dom yg.
    Let g : Monic _ y x₂ := mono_cod_mor yg.

    Let Q₁ : Pullback g s₄ := PB x₂ y x₄ g s₄.
    Let f₁ : Q₁ --> x₃ := PullbackPr2 Q₁ · s₃.

    Let im₁ : C := pr1 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₁).
    Let e₁ : Q₁ --> im₁
      := pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₁).
    Let m₁ : Monic _ im₁ x₃
      := make_Monic _ _ (pr12 (pr222 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₁))).
    Let He₁ : is_strong_epi e₁
      := is_strong_epi_regular_epi
           (pr1 (pr222 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₁))).
    Let p₁ : f₁ = e₁ · m₁
      := pr22 (pr222 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₁)).

    Let f₂ : y --> x₁ := g · s₁.

    Let im₂ : C := pr1 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₂).
    Let e₂ : y --> im₂
      := pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₂).
    Let m₂ : Monic _ im₂ x₁
      := make_Monic _ _ (pr12 (pr222 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₂))).
    Let He₂ : is_regular_epi e₂
      := pr1 (pr222 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₂)).
    Let p₂ : f₂ = e₂ · m₂
      := pr22 (pr222 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₂)).

    Let Q₂ : Pullback m₂ s₂ := PB x₁ im₂ x₃ m₂ s₂.
    Let Q₃ := PB x₁ y x₃ (g · s₁) s₂.

    (**
       To show that dependent sums are stable under pullback in the displayed category
       of all arrows, we use the following morphism. We also use it here.
     *)

g:= mono_cod_mor yg: Monic C y x₂
Q₁:= PB x₂ y x₄ g s₄: Pullback g s₄
f₁:= PullbackPr2 Q₁ · s₃: C ⟦ Q₁, x₃ ⟧
im₁:= pr1
  (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₁): C
e₁:= pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC
        f₁): C ⟦ Q₁, im₁ ⟧
m₁:= make_Monic C
  (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₁))
  (pr122 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
                  HC f₁))): Monic C im₁ x₃
He₁:= is_strong_epi_regular_epi
  (pr122 (pr2
            (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₁))): is_strong_epi e₁
p₁:= pr222 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₁)): f₁ = e₁ · m₁
f₂:= g · s₁: C ⟦ y, x₁ ⟧

  (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₂): C
e₂:= pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC
        f₂): C ⟦ y, im₂ ⟧
m₂:= make_Monic C
  (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₂))

C ⟦ Q₃, y ⟧

PullbackPr1 Q₃ · g =
PullbackArrow P Q₃ (PullbackPr1 Q₃ · g)
  (PullbackPr2 Q₃)
  mono_cod_left_beck_chevalley_mor_inv_subproof · s₄
 abstract
          (exact (!(PullbackArrow_PullbackPr1 P _ _ _ _))).
    Defined.

    (**
       The key idea in the proof is showing that we have a regular epimorphism from
       the pullback `Q₃` to `Q₁`. This permits us to use the lifting property of
       regular epimorphisms.
     *)
    
C: category
HC: is_regular_category C
PB:= is_regular_category_pullbacks HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving PB: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄: C
s₁: C ⟦ x₂, x₁ ⟧
s₂: C ⟦ x₃, x₁ ⟧
s₃: C ⟦ x₄, x₃ ⟧
s₄: C ⟦ x₄, x₂ ⟧
p: s₄ · s₁ = s₃ · s₂
Hp: isPullback p
yg: C /m x₂
P:= make_Pullback p Hp: Pullback s₁ s₂
y:= mono_cod_dom yg: C
g:= mono_cod_mor yg: Monic C y x₂

  (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₁): C
e₁:= pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC
        f₁): C ⟦ Q₁, im₁ ⟧

  (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₂): C

PullbackPr1 Q₃ · e₂ · m₂ = PullbackPr2 Q₃ · s₂
 abstract
          (rewrite !assoc' ;
           rewrite <- p₂ ;
           apply PullbackSqrCommutes).
    Defined.

    (**
       To show that this map is a regular epimorphism, we construct a pullback square
       such that the side opposite to `map_between_pbs` is a regular epimorphism. Then
       by stability of regular epimorphisms (`C` is a regular category), we obtain that
       this morphism is a regular epimorphism.
     *)
    
C: category
HC: is_regular_category C
PB:= is_regular_category_pullbacks HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving PB: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄: C
s₁: C ⟦ x₂, x₁ ⟧
s₂: C ⟦ x₃, x₁ ⟧
s₃: C ⟦ x₄, x₃ ⟧
s₄: C ⟦ x₄, x₂ ⟧
p: s₄ · s₁ = s₃ · s₂
Hp: isPullback p
yg: C /m x₂
P:= make_Pullback p Hp: Pullback s₁ s₂
y:= mono_cod_dom yg: C
g:= mono_cod_mor yg: Monic C y x₂
Q₁:= PB x₂ y x₄ g s₄: Pullback g s₄
f₁:= PullbackPr2 Q₁ · s₃: C ⟦ Q₁, x₃ ⟧
im₁:= pr1
  (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₁): C
e₁:= pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC
        f₁): C ⟦ Q₁, im₁ ⟧
m₁:= make_Monic C
  (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₁))
  (pr122 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
                  HC f₁))): Monic C im₁ x₃
He₁:= is_strong_epi_regular_epi
  (pr122 (pr2
            (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₁))): is_strong_epi e₁
p₁:= pr222 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₁)): f₁ = e₁ · m₁
f₂:= g · s₁: C ⟦ y, x₁ ⟧
im₂:= pr1
  (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₂): C
e₂:= pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC
        f₂): C ⟦ y, im₂ ⟧
m₂:= make_Monic C
  (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₂))
  (pr122 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
                  HC f₂))): Monic C im₂ x₁
He₂:= pr122 (pr2
         (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₂)): is_regular_epi e₂
p₂:= pr222 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₂)): f₂ = e₂ · m₂
Q₂:= PB x₁ im₂ x₃ m₂ s₂: Pullback m₂ s₂
Q₃:= PB x₁ y x₃ (g · s₁) s₂: Pullback (g · s₁) s₂
PullbackPr1 Q₃ · e₂ = map_between_pbs · PullbackPr1 Q₂

    
C: category
HC: is_regular_category C
PB:= is_regular_category_pullbacks HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving PB: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄: C
s₁: C ⟦ x₂, x₁ ⟧
s₂: C ⟦ x₃, x₁ ⟧
s₃: C ⟦ x₄, x₃ ⟧
s₄: C ⟦ x₄, x₂ ⟧
p: s₄ · s₁ = s₃ · s₂
Hp: isPullback p
yg: C /m x₂
P:= make_Pullback p Hp: Pullback s₁ s₂
y:= mono_cod_dom yg: C
g:= mono_cod_mor yg: Monic C y x₂
Q₁:= PB x₂ y x₄ g s₄: Pullback g s₄
f₁:= PullbackPr2 Q₁ · s₃: C ⟦ Q₁, x₃ ⟧
im₁:= pr1
  (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₁): C
e₁:= pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC
        f₁): C ⟦ Q₁, im₁ ⟧
m₁:= make_Monic C
  (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₁))
  (pr122 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
                  HC f₁))): Monic C im₁ x₃
He₁:= is_strong_epi_regular_epi
  (pr122 (pr2
            (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₁))): is_strong_epi e₁
p₁:= pr222 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₁)): f₁ = e₁ · m₁
f₂:= g · s₁: C ⟦ y, x₁ ⟧
im₂:= pr1
  (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₂): C
e₂:= pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC
        f₂): C ⟦ y, im₂ ⟧
m₂:= make_Monic C
  (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₂))
  (pr122 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
                  HC f₂))): Monic C im₂ x₁
He₂:= pr122 (pr2
         (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₂)): is_regular_epi e₂
p₂:= pr222 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₂)): f₂ = e₂ · m₂
Q₂:= PB x₁ im₂ x₃ m₂ s₂: Pullback m₂ s₂
Q₃:= PB x₁ y x₃ (g · s₁) s₂: Pullback (g · s₁) s₂
PullbackPr1 Q₃ · e₂ = map_between_pbs · PullbackPr1 Q₂

               HC f₁))): is_strong_epi e₁
p₁:= pr222 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₁)): f₁ = e₁ · m₁
f₂:= g · s₁: C ⟦ y, x₁ ⟧
im₂:= pr1
  (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₂): C
e₂:= pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC
        f₂): C ⟦ y, im₂ ⟧
m₂:= make_Monic C
  (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₂))
  (pr122 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
                  HC f₂))): Monic C im₂ x₁
He₂:= pr122 (pr2
         (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₂)): is_regular_epi e₂
p₂:= pr222 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₂)): f₂ = e₂ · m₂
Q₂:= PB x₁ im₂ x₃ m₂ s₂: Pullback m₂ s₂
Q₃:= PB x₁ y x₃ (g · s₁) s₂: Pullback (g · s₁) s₂
w: C
h: C ⟦ w, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ w, Q₂ ⟧
r: h · e₂ = k · PullbackPr1 Q₂
ζ₁, ζ₂: ∑ hk : C ⟦ w, Q₃ ⟧,
hk · PullbackPr1 Q₃ = h
× hk · map_between_pbs = k
q:= maponpaths (λ z : C ⟦ w, Q₂ ⟧, z · PullbackPr2 Q₂)
  (pr22 ζ₁ @ ! pr22 ζ₂): (λ z : C ⟦ w, Q₂ ⟧, z · PullbackPr2 Q₂)
  (pr1 ζ₁ · map_between_pbs) =
(λ z : C ⟦ w, Q₂ ⟧, z · PullbackPr2 Q₂)
  (pr1 ζ₂ · map_between_pbs)
pr1 ζ₁ · PullbackPr2 Q₃ = pr1 ζ₂ · PullbackPr2 Q₃

p: s₄ · s₁ = s₃ · s₂

  (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₁): C

m₂:= make_Monic C
  (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₂))
  (pr122 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
                  HC f₂))): Monic C im₂ x₁
He₂:= pr122 (pr2
         (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₂)): is_regular_epi e₂
p₂:= pr222 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₂)): f₂ = e₂ · m₂
Q₂:= PB x₁ im₂ x₃ m₂ s₂: Pullback m₂ s₂
Q₃:= PB x₁ y x₃ (g · s₁) s₂: Pullback (g · s₁) s₂
w: C
h: C ⟦ w, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ w, Q₂ ⟧
r: h · e₂ = k · PullbackPr1 Q₂
is_pb_square_mor · map_between_pbs · PullbackPr2 Q₂ =
k · PullbackPr2 Q₂

C: category

PB:= is_regular_category_pullbacks HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving PB: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄: C
s₁: C ⟦ x₂, x₁ ⟧
s₂: C ⟦ x₃, x₁ ⟧
s₃: C ⟦ x₄, x₃ ⟧
s₄: C ⟦ x₄, x₂ ⟧
p: s₄ · s₁ = s₃ · s₂
Hp: isPullback p
yg: C /m x₂
P:= make_Pullback p Hp: Pullback s₁ s₂
y:= mono_cod_dom yg: C
g:= mono_cod_mor yg: Monic C y x₂
Q₁:= PB x₂ y x₄ g s₄: Pullback g s₄
f₁:= PullbackPr2 Q₁ · s₃: C ⟦ Q₁, x₃ ⟧
im₁:= pr1
  (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₁): C
e₁:= pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC
        f₁): C ⟦ Q₁, im₁ ⟧
m₁:= make_Monic C
  (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₁))
  (pr122 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
                  HC f₁))): Monic C im₁ x₃
He₁:= is_strong_epi_regular_epi
  (pr122 (pr2
            (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₁))): is_strong_epi e₁
p₁:= pr222 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₁)): f₁ = e₁ · m₁
f₂:= g · s₁: C ⟦ y, x₁ ⟧
im₂:= pr1
  (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₂): C
e₂:= pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC
        f₂): C ⟦ y, im₂ ⟧
m₂:= make_Monic C
  (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₂))
  (pr122 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
                  HC f₂))): Monic C im₂ x₁
He₂:= pr122 (pr2
         (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₂)): is_regular_epi e₂
p₂:= pr222 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₂)): f₂ = e₂ · m₂
Q₂:= PB x₁ im₂ x₃ m₂ s₂: Pullback m₂ s₂
Q₃:= PB x₁ y x₃ (g · s₁) s₂: Pullback (g · s₁) s₂
w: C
h: C ⟦ w, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ w, Q₂ ⟧
r: h · e₂ = k · PullbackPr1 Q₂
PullbackArrow Q₃ w h (k · PullbackPr2 Q₂)
  is_pb_square_mor_subproof
· (PullbackArrow Q₂ Q₃ (PullbackPr1 Q₃ · e₂)
     (PullbackPr2 Q₃) map_between_pbs_subproof
   · PullbackPr2 Q₂) = k · PullbackPr2 Q₂

          
C: category
HC: is_regular_category C
PB:= is_regular_category_pullbacks HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving PB: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄: C
s₁: C ⟦ x₂, x₁ ⟧
s₂: C ⟦ x₃, x₁ ⟧
s₃: C ⟦ x₄, x₃ ⟧
s₄: C ⟦ x₄, x₂ ⟧
p: s₄ · s₁ = s₃ · s₂
Hp: isPullback p
yg: C /m x₂
P:= make_Pullback p Hp: Pullback s₁ s₂
y:= mono_cod_dom yg: C
g:= mono_cod_mor yg: Monic C y x₂
Q₁:= PB x₂ y x₄ g s₄: Pullback g s₄
f₁:= PullbackPr2 Q₁ · s₃: C ⟦ Q₁, x₃ ⟧
im₁:= pr1
  (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₁): C
e₁:= pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC
        f₁): C ⟦ Q₁, im₁ ⟧
m₁:= make_Monic C
  (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₁))
  (pr122 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
                  HC f₁))): Monic C im₁ x₃
He₁:= is_strong_epi_regular_epi
  (pr122 (pr2
            (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₁))): is_strong_epi e₁
p₁:= pr222 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₁)): f₁ = e₁ · m₁
f₂:= g · s₁: C ⟦ y, x₁ ⟧
im₂:= pr1
  (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₂): C
e₂:= pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC
        f₂): C ⟦ y, im₂ ⟧
m₂:= make_Monic C
  (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₂))
  (pr122 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
                  HC f₂))): Monic C im₂ x₁
He₂:= pr122 (pr2
         (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₂)): is_regular_epi e₂
p₂:= pr222 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₂)): f₂ = e₂ · m₂
Q₂:= PB x₁ im₂ x₃ m₂ s₂: Pullback m₂ s₂
Q₃:= PB x₁ y x₃ (g · s₁) s₂: Pullback (g · s₁) s₂
w: C
h: C ⟦ w, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ w, Q₂ ⟧
r: h · e₂ = k · PullbackPr1 Q₂
k · PullbackPr2 Q₂ = k · PullbackPr2 Q₂

          apply idpath.
      Qed.
    End UMP.

HC: is_regular_category C
PB:= is_regular_category_pullbacks HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving PB: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄: C
s₁: C ⟦ x₂, x₁ ⟧
s₂: C ⟦ x₃, x₁ ⟧
s₃: C ⟦ x₄, x₃ ⟧
s₄: C ⟦ x₄, x₂ ⟧
p: s₄ · s₁ = s₃ · s₂
Hp: isPullback p
yg: C /m x₂
P:= make_Pullback p Hp: Pullback s₁ s₂
y:= mono_cod_dom yg: C
g:= mono_cod_mor yg: Monic C y x₂
Q₁:= PB x₂ y x₄ g s₄: Pullback g s₄
f₁:= PullbackPr2 Q₁ · s₃: C ⟦ Q₁, x₃ ⟧
im₁:= pr1
  (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₁): C
e₁:= pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC
        f₁): C ⟦ Q₁, im₁ ⟧
m₁:= make_Monic C
  (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₁))
  (pr122 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
                  HC f₁))): Monic C im₁ x₃
He₁:= is_strong_epi_regular_epi
  (pr122 (pr2
            (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₁))): is_strong_epi e₁
p₁:= pr222 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₁)): f₁ = e₁ · m₁
f₂:= g · s₁: C ⟦ y, x₁ ⟧
im₂:= pr1
  (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₂): C
e₂:= pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC
        f₂): C ⟦ y, im₂ ⟧
m₂:= make_Monic C
  (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₂))
  (pr122 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
                  HC f₂))): Monic C im₂ x₁
He₂:= pr122 (pr2
         (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₂)): is_regular_epi e₂
p₂:= pr222 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₂)): f₂ = e₂ · m₂
Q₂:= PB x₁ im₂ x₃ m₂ s₂: Pullback m₂ s₂
Q₃:= PB x₁ y x₃ (g · s₁) s₂: Pullback (g · s₁) s₂
w: C
h: C ⟦ w, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ w, Q₂ ⟧
r: h · e₂ = k · PullbackPr1 Q₂
∃! hk : C ⟦ w, Q₃ ⟧,
hk · PullbackPr1 Q₃ = h × hk · map_between_pbs = k

               HC f₁))): is_strong_epi e₁
p₁:= pr222 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₁)): f₁ = e₁ · m₁
f₂:= g · s₁: C ⟦ y, x₁ ⟧
im₂:= pr1
  (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₂): C
e₂:= pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC
        f₂): C ⟦ y, im₂ ⟧
m₂:= make_Monic C
  (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₂))
  (pr122 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
                  HC f₂))): Monic C im₂ x₁
He₂:= pr122 (pr2
         (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₂)): is_regular_epi e₂
p₂:= pr222 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₂)): f₂ = e₂ · m₂
Q₂:= PB x₁ im₂ x₃ m₂ s₂: Pullback m₂ s₂
Q₃:= PB x₁ y x₃ (g · s₁) s₂: Pullback (g · s₁) s₂
w: C
h: C ⟦ w, y ⟧
k: C ⟦ w, Q₂ ⟧
r: h · e₂ = k · PullbackPr1 Q₂
∑ hk : C ⟦ w, Q₃ ⟧,
hk · PullbackPr1 Q₃ = h × hk · map_between_pbs = k

s₂: C ⟦ x₃, x₁ ⟧
s₃: C ⟦ x₄, x₃ ⟧
s₄: C ⟦ x₄, x₂ ⟧
p: s₄ · s₁ = s₃ · s₂
Hp: isPullback p
yg: C /m x₂
P:= make_Pullback p Hp: Pullback s₁ s₂
y:= mono_cod_dom yg: C
g:= mono_cod_mor yg: Monic C y x₂
Q₁:= PB x₂ y x₄ g s₄: Pullback g s₄
f₁:= PullbackPr2 Q₁ · s₃: C ⟦ Q₁, x₃ ⟧
im₁:= pr1
  (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₁): C
e₁:= pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC
        f₁): C ⟦ Q₁, im₁ ⟧
m₁:= make_Monic C
  (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₁))
  (pr122 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
                  HC f₁))): Monic C im₁ x₃
He₁:= is_strong_epi_regular_epi
  (pr122 (pr2
            (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₁))): is_strong_epi e₁
p₁:= pr222 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₁)): f₁ = e₁ · m₁
f₂:= g · s₁: C ⟦ y, x₁ ⟧
im₂:= pr1
  (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₂): C
e₂:= pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC
        f₂): C ⟦ y, im₂ ⟧
m₂:= make_Monic C
  (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₂))
  (pr122 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
                  HC f₂))): Monic C im₂ x₁
He₂:= pr122 (pr2
         (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₂)): is_regular_epi e₂
p₂:= pr222 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₂)): f₂ = e₂ · m₂
Q₂:= PB x₁ im₂ x₃ m₂ s₂: Pullback m₂ s₂
Q₃:= PB x₁ y x₃ (g · s₁) s₂: Pullback (g · s₁) s₂
is_regular_epi map_between_pbs

      exact (is_regular_category_regular_epi_pb_stable
               HC
               _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _
               is_pb_square
               He₂).
    Qed.

    (**
       Now we consider the following square

<<
                                 e₁
        Q₃ -------------> Q₁ --------> im₁
        |                              |
        |                              | m₁
        |                              |
        V                              V
        Q₂ --------------------------> x₃
>>

       The map `Q₁ --> Q₂` is `map_between_pbs`, which is a regular
       epimorphism. The map `Q₂ --> x₃` is a pullback projection, and
       `mono_cod_left_beck_chevalley_mor_inv` is the moprhism from `Q₃`
       to `Q₁`. By showing that this diagram commutes, we can use the
       lifting property of regular epimorphisms with respect to
       monomorphism to obtain a map `Q₂ --> im₁` making the triangles
       commute. From this we can directly conclude the stability under
       pullback of existential quantification.
     *)
    
C: category
HC: is_regular_category C
PB:= is_regular_category_pullbacks HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving PB: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄: C
s₁: C ⟦ x₂, x₁ ⟧
s₂: C ⟦ x₃, x₁ ⟧
s₃: C ⟦ x₄, x₃ ⟧
s₄: C ⟦ x₄, x₂ ⟧
p: s₄ · s₁ = s₃ · s₂
Hp: isPullback p
yg: C /m x₂
P:= make_Pullback p Hp: Pullback s₁ s₂
y:= mono_cod_dom yg: C
g:= mono_cod_mor yg: Monic C y x₂
Q₁:= PB x₂ y x₄ g s₄: Pullback g s₄
f₁:= PullbackPr2 Q₁ · s₃: C ⟦ Q₁, x₃ ⟧
im₁:= pr1
  (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₁): C
e₁:= pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC
        f₁): C ⟦ Q₁, im₁ ⟧
m₁:= make_Monic C
  (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₁))
  (pr122 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
                  HC f₁))): Monic C im₁ x₃
He₁:= is_strong_epi_regular_epi
  (pr122 (pr2
            (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₁))): is_strong_epi e₁
p₁:= pr222 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₁)): f₁ = e₁ · m₁
f₂:= g · s₁: C ⟦ y, x₁ ⟧
im₂:= pr1
  (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC f₂): C
e₂:= pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC
        f₂): C ⟦ y, im₂ ⟧
m₂:= make_Monic C
  (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₂))
  (pr122 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
                  HC f₂))): Monic C im₂ x₁
He₂:= pr122 (pr2
         (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
            HC f₂)): is_regular_epi e₂
p₂:= pr222 (pr22 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
               HC f₂)): f₂ = e₂ · m₂
Q₂:= PB x₁ im₂ x₃ m₂ s₂: Pullback m₂ s₂
Q₃:= PB x₁ y x₃ (g · s₁) s₂: Pullback (g · s₁) s₂
map_between_pbs · PullbackPr2 Q₂ =
mono_cod_left_beck_chevalley_mor_inv · e₁ · m₁

  (PullbackPr2 Q₃) map_between_pbs_subproof
· PullbackPr2 Q₂ =

∏ (Γ₁ Γ₂ Γ₃ Γ₄ : C) (s₁ : C ⟦ Γ₂, Γ₁ ⟧)
(s₂ : C ⟦ Γ₃, Γ₁ ⟧) (s₃ : C ⟦ Γ₄, Γ₃ ⟧)
(s₄ : C ⟦ Γ₄, Γ₂ ⟧) (p : s₄ · s₁ = s₃ · s₂),
isPullback p
→ ∏
  φ : Fiber.fiber_category (disp_mono_codomain C) Γ₂,
  pr1 (HD Γ₁ Γ₃ s₂ (?ex Γ₂ Γ₁ s₁ φ)) -->[
  identity Γ₃] ?ex Γ₄ Γ₃ s₃ (pr1 (HD Γ₂ Γ₄ s₄ φ))

    
C: category
HC: is_regular_category C
PB:= is_regular_category_pullbacks HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving PB: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
locally_propositional (disp_mono_codomain C)
 apply locally_propositional_mono_cod_disp_cat.
    
C: category
HC: is_regular_category C
PB:= is_regular_category_pullbacks HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving PB: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
∏ Γ₁ Γ₂ : C,
C ⟦ Γ₁, Γ₂ ⟧
→ Fiber.fiber_category (disp_mono_codomain C) Γ₁
  → Fiber.fiber_category (disp_mono_codomain C) Γ₂
 exact (λ y₁ y₂ f xg, mono_codomain_exists f xg).
    
C: category
HC: is_regular_category C
PB:= is_regular_category_pullbacks HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving PB: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
∏ (Γ₁ Γ₂ : C) (s : C ⟦ Γ₁, Γ₂ ⟧)
(φ : Fiber.fiber_category (disp_mono_codomain C) Γ₁),
φ -->[
identity Γ₁] pr1
               (HD Γ₂ Γ₁ s
                  ((λ (y₁ y₂ : C) (f : C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧)
                    (xg : Fiber.fiber_category
                            (disp_mono_codomain C) y₁),
                    mono_codomain_exists f xg) Γ₁ Γ₂ s
                     φ))
 exact (λ y₁ y₂ f xg, mono_codomain_exists_intro f xg).
    
C: category
HC: is_regular_category C
PB:= is_regular_category_pullbacks HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving PB: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
∏ (Γ₁ Γ₂ : C) (s : C ⟦ Γ₁, Γ₂ ⟧)
(ψ : Fiber.fiber_category (disp_mono_codomain C) Γ₁)
(χ : Fiber.fiber_category (disp_mono_codomain C) Γ₂),
ψ -->[ identity Γ₁] pr1 (HD Γ₂ Γ₁ s χ)
→ (λ (y₁ y₂ : C) (f : C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧)
   (xg : Fiber.fiber_category (disp_mono_codomain C)
           y₁), mono_codomain_exists f xg) Γ₁ Γ₂ s ψ -->[
  identity Γ₂] χ

HC: is_regular_category C
PB:= is_regular_category_pullbacks HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving PB: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
Γ₁, Γ₂: C
s: C ⟦ Γ₁, Γ₂ ⟧
ψ: Fiber.fiber_category (disp_mono_codomain C) Γ₁
χ: Fiber.fiber_category (disp_mono_codomain C) Γ₂
p: ψ -->[ identity Γ₁] pr1 (HD Γ₂ Γ₁ s χ)

 (xg : Fiber.fiber_category (disp_mono_codomain C) y₁),
 mono_codomain_exists f xg) Γ₁ Γ₂ s ψ -->[
identity Γ₂] χ

C /m Γ₁ ⟦ ψ, mono_cod_pb PB s χ ⟧

      exact p.
    
C: category
HC: is_regular_category C
PB:= is_regular_category_pullbacks HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving PB: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
∏ (Γ₁ Γ₂ Γ₃ Γ₄ : C) (s₁ : C ⟦ Γ₂, Γ₁ ⟧)
(s₂ : C ⟦ Γ₃, Γ₁ ⟧) (s₃ : C ⟦ Γ₄, Γ₃ ⟧)
(s₄ : C ⟦ Γ₄, Γ₂ ⟧) (p : s₄ · s₁ = s₃ · s₂),
isPullback p
→ ∏
  φ : Fiber.fiber_category (disp_mono_codomain C) Γ₂,
  pr1
    (HD Γ₁ Γ₃ s₂
       ((λ (y₁ y₂ : C) (f : C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧)
         (xg : Fiber.fiber_category
                 (disp_mono_codomain C) y₁),
         mono_codomain_exists f xg) Γ₂ Γ₁ s₁ φ)) -->[
  identity Γ₃] (λ (y₁ y₂ : C) (f : C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧)
                (xg : Fiber.fiber_category
                        (disp_mono_codomain C) y₁),
                mono_codomain_exists f xg) Γ₄ Γ₃ s₃
                 (pr1 (HD Γ₂ Γ₄ s₄ φ))
 
C: category
HC: is_regular_category C
PB:= is_regular_category_pullbacks HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving PB: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
x₁, x₂, x₃, x₄: C
s₁: C ⟦ x₂, x₁ ⟧
s₂: C ⟦ x₃, x₁ ⟧
s₃: C ⟦ x₄, x₃ ⟧
s₄: C ⟦ x₄, x₂ ⟧
p: s₄ · s₁ = s₃ · s₂
Hp: isPullback p
yg: Fiber.fiber_category (disp_mono_codomain C) x₂
pr1
  (HD x₁ x₃ s₂
     ((λ (y₁ y₂ : C) (f : C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧)
       (xg : Fiber.fiber_category
               (disp_mono_codomain C) y₁),
       mono_codomain_exists f xg) x₂ x₁ s₁ yg)) -->[
identity x₃] (λ (y₁ y₂ : C) (f : C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧)
              (xg : Fiber.fiber_category
                      (disp_mono_codomain C) y₁),
              mono_codomain_exists f xg) x₄ x₃ s₃
               (pr1 (HD x₂ x₄ s₄ yg))

      exact (mono_codomain_exists_stable Hp yg).
  Defined.
End MonoCodomainLeftAdj.
